msg:This price is great value for money. I live in a duplex holiday home with two floors. There is a lake outside the first floor, and you can go to the lake. The bed is on the first floor, with a large bed and a bunk bed, which is just right for a family of four. The bathtub is large and deep, and the water drains quickly. There is a balcony on the second floor. It is very comfortable to sunbathe when the weather is good. There is also a clothes drying rack. It would be better if there is a table and stool. The house is fully equipped with microwave ovens, refrigerators, tableware, capsule coffee machines, and children's things are also very thoughtful, such as footstools and toilet seats. The outdoor area is very open and the children's playground is very fun. You can also play basketball and football. If the weather is good, I strongly recommend staying here. The only drawback is that I live in a two-story building. After turning on the air conditioner, the temperature difference between the second floor and the first floor is very large.

This can be repaired or replaced when it is found to be broken during cleaning, otherwise the velvet will leak and the children can't play with it, so it's better not to put it; the sanitation of the room is not ideal, so we wiped it again ourselves. The sewer has a very strong odor, and I couldn't sleep at 5 o'clock in the morning.
Play: It's hot and I didn't play outdoors, so I won't comment for the time being. The swimming pool is still very good, more suitable for young children. It's just that the opening time is 12 o'clock, I don't understand why.
Service: It can be said that there is no service. Except for the shuttle bus master who helped to take the luggage in the parking lot, I didn't feel any service from check-in to check-out. We needed dinner delivery. We searched the room and found no delivery menu. We called the front desk to ask where the delivery menu was in the room. They said it was there and asked us to look for it carefully. They also told us that we could deliver the food before 23:00. Without a menu, we could only ask the restaurant if they could deliver the food or send us a menu first. The restaurant replied that they could only deliver the food at 20:00...otherwise, we could only eat it ourselves. I was speechless. First of all, is there no unified statement about the delivery time in the entire resort? Second, is 8 o'clock in the evening a reasonable dinner time? They also kept emphasizing that the flowers delivered would require a 10% service charge. I just want to ask where the service is? No one at the front desk or the restaurant even delivered a menu. Finally, I called the front desk again and a girl delivered it, otherwise I would not want to comment at all.
Meals: Although the delivery process was unpleasant, the food delivered in the end was still okay. There were not many varieties of breakfast the next day, but it was enough. We went there at 7:30, and somehow the floor was full of water, which was very easy to slip. The service staff kept coming to collect the plates before we finished the meal.
We wanted to stay another day if the stay was okay, but we left immediately after breakfast. We didn't want to stay even a minute longer.
We just came back from another family hotel the day before yesterday, and the service was so different. If the service awareness is not improved, it will be difficult to compete. If it is only a one-time business, it will be ignored. The real feeling is that I will not come again anyway.
